    13	func RichParameter(inv *serpent.Invocation, templateVersionParameter codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter, defaultOverrides map[string]string) (string, error) {
    14	        label := templateVersionParameter.Name
    15	        if templateVersionParameter.DisplayName != "" {
    16	                label = templateVersionParameter.DisplayName
    17	        }
    18	
    19	        if templateVersionParameter.Ephemeral {
    20	                label += pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Warn, " (build option)")
    21	        }
    22	
    23	        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, Bold(label))
    24	
    25	        if templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext != "" {
    26	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, "  "+strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(strings.Split(templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext, "\n"), "\n  "))+"\n")
    27	        }
    28	
    29	        defaultValue := templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue
    30	        if v, ok := defaultOverrides[templateVersionParameter.Name]; ok {
    31	                defaultValue = v
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        var err error
    35	        var value string
    36	        switch {
    37	        case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
    38	                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
    39	                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
    40	
    41	                var options []string
    42	                err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &options)
    43	                if err != nil {
    44	                        return "", err
    45	                }
    46	
    47	                values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
    48	                        Options:  options,
    49	                        Defaults: options,
    50	                })
    51	                if err == nil {
    52	                        v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
    53	                        if err != nil {
    54	                                return "", err
    55	                        }
    56	
    57	                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
    58	                        pretty.Fprintf(
    59	                                inv.Stdout,
    60	                                DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
    61	                        )
    62	                        value = string(v)
    63	                }
    64	        case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:
    65	                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
    66	                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
    67	                var richParameterOption *codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
    68	                richParameterOption, err = RichSelect(inv, RichSelectOptions{
    69	                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
    70	                        Default:    defaultValue,
    71	                        HideSearch: true,
    72	                })
    73	                if err == nil {
    74	                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
    75	                        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
    76	                        value = richParameterOption.Value
    77	                }
    78	        default:
    79	                text := "Enter a value"
    80	                if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
    81	                        text += fmt.Sprintf(" (default: %q)", defaultValue)
    82	                }
    83	                text += ":"
    84	
    85	                value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
    86	                        Text: Bold(text),
    87	                        Validate: func(value string) error {
    88	                                return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
    89	                        },
    90	                })
    91	                value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
    92	        }
    93	        if err != nil {
    94	                return "", err
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        // If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
    98	        if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == "" {
    99	                value = defaultValue
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        return value, nil
   103	}
   104	
   105	func validateRichPrompt(value string, p codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter) error {
   106	        return codersdk.ValidateWorkspaceBuildParameter(p, &codersdk.WorkspaceBuildParameter{
   107	                Name:  p.Name,
   108	                Value: value,
   109	        }, nil)
   110	}

     1	package cliui
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "flag"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "os"
     7	        "os/signal"

     9	        "syscall"

    11	        "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbles/textinput"
    12	        tea "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbletea"
    13	        "golang.org/x/xerrors"

    19	
    20	const defaultSelectModelHeight = 7
    21	
    22	type terminateMsg struct{}
    23	
    24	func installSignalHandler(p *tea.Program) func() {
    25	        ch := make(chan struct{})
    26	
    27	        go func() {
    28	                sig := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    29	                signal.Notify(sig, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)
    30	
    31	                defer func() {
    32	                        signal.Stop(sig)
    33	                        close(ch)
    34	                }()
    35	
    36	                for {
    37	                        select {
    38	                        case <-ch:
    39	                                return
    40	
    41	                        case <-sig:
    42	                                p.Send(terminateMsg{})
    43	                        }
    44	                }
    45	        }()
    46	
    47	        return func() {
    48	                ch <- struct{}{}
    49	        }
    50	}
    51	
    52	type SelectOptions struct {
    53	        Options []string
    54	        // Default will be highlighted first if it's a valid option.
    55	        Default    string
    56	        Message    string
    57	        Size       int
    58	        HideSearch bool
    59	}
    60	
    61	type RichSelectOptions struct {
    62	        Options    []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
    63	        Default    string
    64	        Size       int
    65	        HideSearch bool
    66	}
    67	
    68	// RichSelect displays a list of user options including name and description.
    69	func RichSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichSelectOptions) (*codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption, error) {
    70	        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
    71	        var defaultOpt string
    72	        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
    73	                line := option.Name
    74	                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
    75	                        line += ": " + option.Description
    76	                }
    77	                opts[i] = line
    78	
    79	                if option.Value == richOptions.Default {
    80	                        defaultOpt = line
    81	                }
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        selected, err := Select(inv, SelectOptions{
    85	                Options:    opts,
    86	                Default:    defaultOpt,
    87	                Size:       richOptions.Size,
    88	                HideSearch: richOptions.HideSearch,
    89	        })
    90	        if err != nil {
    91	                return nil, err
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        for i, option := range opts {
    95	                if option == selected {
    96	                        return &richOptions.Options[i], nil
    97	                }
    98	        }
    99	        return nil, xerrors.Errorf("unknown option selected: %s", selected)
   100	}
   101	
   102	// Select displays a list of user options.
   103	func Select(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts SelectOptions) (string, error) {
   104	        // The survey library used *always* fails when testing on Windows,
   105	        // as it requires a live TTY (can't be a conpty). We should fork
   106	        // this library to add a dummy fallback, that simply reads/writes
   107	        // to the IO provided. See:
   108	        // https://github.com/AlecAivazis/survey/blob/master/terminal/runereader_windows.go#L94
   109	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   110	                return opts.Options[0], nil
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        initialModel := selectModel{
   114	                search:     textinput.New(),
   115	                hideSearch: opts.HideSearch,
   116	                options:    opts.Options,
   117	                height:     opts.Size,
   118	                message:    opts.Message,
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        if initialModel.height == 0 {
   122	                initialModel.height = defaultSelectModelHeight
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   126	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   127	
   128	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   129	                initialModel,
   130	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   131	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   132	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   133	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   134	        )
   135	
   136	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   137	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   138	
   139	        m, err := p.Run()
   140	        if err != nil {
   141	                return "", err
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        model, ok := m.(selectModel)
   145	        if !ok {
   146	                return "", xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        if model.canceled {
   150	                return "", ErrCanceled
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        return model.selected, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	type selectModel struct {
   157	        search     textinput.Model
   158	        options    []string
   159	        cursor     int
   160	        height     int
   161	        message    string
   162	        selected   string
   163	        canceled   bool
   164	        hideSearch bool
   165	}
   166	
   167	func (selectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   168	        return nil
   169	}
   170	
   171	//nolint:revive // The linter complains about modifying 'm' but this is typical practice for bubbletea
   172	func (m selectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   173	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   174	
   175	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   176	        case terminateMsg:
   177	                m.canceled = true
   178	                return m, tea.Quit
   179	
   180	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   181	                switch msg.Type {
   182	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   183	                        m.canceled = true
   184	                        return m, tea.Quit
   185	
   186	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   187	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   188	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   189	                                m.selected = options[m.cursor]
   190	                                return m, tea.Quit
   191	                        }
   192	
   193	                case tea.KeyUp:
   194	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   195	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   196	                                m.cursor--
   197	                        } else {
   198	                                m.cursor = len(options) - 1
   199	                        }
   200	
   201	                case tea.KeyDown:
   202	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   203	                        if m.cursor < len(options)-1 {
   204	                                m.cursor++
   205	                        } else {
   206	                                m.cursor = 0
   207	                        }
   208	                }
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        if !m.hideSearch {
   212	                oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   213	                m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   214	
   215	                // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   216	                // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   217	                if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   218	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   219	
   220	                        if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   221	                                m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   222	                        }
   223	                }
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        return m, cmd
   227	}
   228	
   229	func (m selectModel) View() string {
   230	        var s strings.Builder
   231	
   232	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   233	
   234	        if m.selected != "" {
   235	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, m.selected)
   236	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   237	
   238	                return s.String()
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        if m.hideSearch {
   242	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s [Use arrows to move]\n", msg))
   243	        } else {
   244	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   245	                        "%s %s[Use arrows to move, type to filter]\n",
   246	                        msg,
   247	                        m.search.View(),
   248	                ))
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        options, start := m.viewableOptions()
   252	
   253	        for i, option := range options {
   254	                // Is this the currently selected option?
   255	                style := pretty.Wrap("  ", "")
   256	                if m.cursor == start+i {
   257	                        style = pretty.Style{
   258	                                pretty.Wrap("> ", ""),
   259	                                DefaultStyles.Keyword,
   260	                        }
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                _, _ = s.WriteString(pretty.Sprint(style, option))
   264	                _, _ = s.WriteString("\n")
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        return s.String()
   268	}
   269	
   270	func (m selectModel) viewableOptions() ([]string, int) {
   271	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   272	        halfHeight := m.height / 2
   273	        bottom := 0
   274	        top := len(options)
   275	
   276	        switch {
   277	        case m.cursor <= halfHeight:
   278	                top = min(top, m.height)
   279	        case m.cursor < top-halfHeight:
   280	                bottom = max(0, m.cursor-halfHeight)
   281	                top = min(top, m.cursor+halfHeight+1)
   282	        default:
   283	                bottom = max(0, top-m.height)
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return options[bottom:top], bottom
   287	}
   288	
   289	func (m selectModel) filteredOptions() []string {
   290	        options := []string{}
   291	        for _, o := range m.options {
   292	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   293	                option := strings.ToLower(o)
   294	
   295	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   296	                        options = append(options, o)
   297	                }
   298	        }
   299	        return options
   300	}
   301	
   302	type MultiSelectOptions struct {
   303	        Message           string
   304	        Options           []string
   305	        Defaults          []string
   306	        EnableCustomInput bool
   307	}
   308	
   309	func MultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts MultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
   310	        // Similar hack is applied to Select()
   311	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   312	                return opts.Defaults, nil
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        options := make([]*multiSelectOption, len(opts.Options))
   316	        for i, option := range opts.Options {
   317	                chosen := false
   318	                for _, d := range opts.Defaults {
   319	                        if option == d {
   320	                                chosen = true
   321	                                break
   322	                        }
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                options[i] = &multiSelectOption{
   326	                        option: option,
   327	                        chosen: chosen,
   328	                }
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        initialModel := multiSelectModel{
   332	                search:            textinput.New(),
   333	                options:           options,
   334	                message:           opts.Message,
   335	                enableCustomInput: opts.EnableCustomInput,
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   339	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   340	
   341	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   342	                initialModel,
   343	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   344	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   345	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   346	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   347	        )
   348	
   349	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   350	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   351	
   352	        m, err := p.Run()
   353	        if err != nil {
   354	                return nil, err
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
   358	        if !ok {
   359	                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        if model.canceled {
   363	                return nil, ErrCanceled
   364	        }
   365	
   366	        return model.selectedOptions(), nil
   367	}
   368	
   369	type multiSelectOption struct {
   370	        option string
   371	        chosen bool
   372	}
   373	
   374	type multiSelectModel struct {
   375	        search            textinput.Model
   376	        options           []*multiSelectOption
   377	        cursor            int
   378	        message           string
   379	        canceled          bool
   380	        selected          bool
   381	        isCustomInputMode bool   // track if we're adding a custom option
   382	        customInput       string // store custom input
   383	        enableCustomInput bool   // control whether custom input is allowed
   384	}
   385	
   386	func (multiSelectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   387	        return nil
   388	}
   389	
   390	//nolint:revive // For same reason as previous Update definition
   391	func (m multiSelectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   392	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   393	
   394	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   395	                return m.handleCustomInputMode(msg)
   396	        }
   397	
   398	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   399	        case terminateMsg:
   400	                m.canceled = true
   401	                return m, tea.Quit
   402	
   403	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   404	                switch msg.Type {
   405	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   406	                        m.canceled = true
   407	                        return m, tea.Quit
   408	
   409	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   410	                        // Switch to custom input mode if we're on the "+ Add custom value:" option
   411	                        if m.enableCustomInput && m.cursor == len(m.filteredOptions()) {
   412	                                m.isCustomInputMode = true
   413	                                return m, nil
   414	                        }
   415	                        if len(m.options) != 0 {
   416	                                m.selected = true
   417	                                return m, tea.Quit
   418	                        }
   419	
   420	                case tea.KeySpace:
   421	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   422	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   423	                                options[m.cursor].chosen = !options[m.cursor].chosen
   424	                        }
   425	                        // We back out early here otherwise a space will be inserted
   426	                        // into the search field.
   427	                        return m, nil
   428	
   429	                case tea.KeyUp:
   430	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   431	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   432	                                m.cursor--
   433	                        } else {
   434	                                m.cursor = maxIndex
   435	                        }
   436	
   437	                case tea.KeyDown:
   438	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   439	                        if m.cursor < maxIndex {
   440	                                m.cursor++
   441	                        } else {
   442	                                m.cursor = 0
   443	                        }
   444	
   445	                case tea.KeyRight:
   446	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   447	                        for _, option := range options {
   448	                                option.chosen = true
   449	                        }
   450	
   451	                case tea.KeyLeft:
   452	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   453	                        for _, option := range options {
   454	                                option.chosen = false
   455	                        }
   456	                }
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   460	        m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   461	
   462	        // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   463	        // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   464	        if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   465	                options := m.filteredOptions()
   466	                if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   467	                        m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   468	                }
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        return m, cmd
   472	}
   473	
   474	func (m multiSelectModel) getMaxIndex() int {
   475	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   476	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   477	                // Include the "+ Add custom value" entry
   478	                return len(options)
   479	        }
   480	        // Includes only the actual options
   481	        return len(options) - 1
   482	}
   483	
   484	// handleCustomInputMode manages keyboard interactions when in custom input mode
   485	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputMode(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   486	        keyMsg, ok := msg.(tea.KeyMsg)
   487	        if !ok {
   488	                return m, nil
   489	        }
   490	
   491	        switch keyMsg.Type {
   492	        case tea.KeyEnter:
   493	                return m.handleCustomInputSubmission()
   494	
   495	        case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   496	                m.canceled = true
   497	                return m, tea.Quit
   498	
   499	        case tea.KeyBackspace:
   500	                return m.handleCustomInputBackspace()
   501	
   502	        default:
   503	                m.customInput += keyMsg.String()
   504	                return m, nil
   505	        }
   506	}
   507	
   508	// handleCustomInputSubmission processes the submission of custom input
   509	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputSubmission() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   510	        if m.customInput == "" {
   511	                m.isCustomInputMode = false
   512	                return m, nil
   513	        }
   514	
   515	        // Clear search to ensure option is visible and cursor points to the new option
   516	        m.search.SetValue("")
   517	
   518	        // Check for duplicates
   519	        for i, opt := range m.options {
   520	                if opt.option == m.customInput {
   521	                        // If the option exists but isn't chosen, select it
   522	                        if !opt.chosen {
   523	                                opt.chosen = true
   524	                        }
   525	
   526	                        // Point cursor to the new option
   527	                        m.cursor = i
   528	
   529	                        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   530	                        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   531	                        m.customInput = ""
   532	                        return m, nil
   533	                }
   534	        }
   535	
   536	        // Add new unique option
   537	        m.options = append(m.options, &multiSelectOption{
   538	                option: m.customInput,
   539	                chosen: true,
   540	        })
   541	
   542	        // Point cursor to the newly added option
   543	        m.cursor = len(m.options) - 1
   544	
   545	        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   546	        m.customInput = ""
   547	        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   548	        return m, nil
   549	}
   550	
   551	// handleCustomInputBackspace handles backspace in custom input mode
   552	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputBackspace() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   553	        if len(m.customInput) > 0 {
   554	                m.customInput = m.customInput[:len(m.customInput)-1]
   555	        }
   556	        return m, nil
   557	}
   558	
   559	func (m multiSelectModel) View() string {
   560	        var s strings.Builder
   561	
   562	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   563	
   564	        if m.selected {
   565	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, strings.Join(m.selectedOptions(), ", "))
   566	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   567	
   568	                return s.String()
   569	        }
   570	
   571	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   572	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s\nEnter custom value: %s\n", msg, m.customInput))
   573	                return s.String()
   574	        }
   575	
   576	        _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   577	                "%s %s[Use arrows to move, space to select, <right> to all, <left> to none, type to filter]\n",
   578	                msg,
   579	                m.search.View(),
   580	        ))
   581	
   582	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   583	        for i, option := range options {
   584	                cursor := "  "
   585	                chosen := "[ ]"
   586	                o := option.option
   587	
   588	                if m.cursor == i {
   589	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   590	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[ ]")
   591	                        o = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, o)
   592	                }
   593	
   594	                if option.chosen {
   595	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[x]")
   596	                }
   597	
   598	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   599	                        "%s%s %s\n",
   600	                        cursor,
   601	                        chosen,
   602	                        o,
   603	                ))
   604	        }
   605	
   606	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   607	                // Add the "+ Add custom value" option at the bottom
   608	                cursor := "  "
   609	                text := " + Add custom value"
   610	                if m.cursor == len(options) {
   611	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   612	                        text = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, text)
   613	                }
   614	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s%s\n", cursor, text))
   615	        }
   616	        return s.String()
   617	}
   618	
   619	func (m multiSelectModel) filteredOptions() []*multiSelectOption {
   620	        options := []*multiSelectOption{}
   621	        for _, o := range m.options {
   622	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   623	                option := strings.ToLower(o.option)
   624	
   625	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   626	                        options = append(options, o)
   627	                }
   628	        }
   629	        return options
   630	}
   631	
   632	func (m multiSelectModel) selectedOptions() []string {
   633	        selected := []string{}
   634	        for _, o := range m.options {
   635	                if o.chosen {
   636	                        selected = append(selected, o.option)
   637	                }
   638	        }
   639	        return selected
   640	}

// This is a minimal repro for the two bugs described:
// 1) list(string) MultiSelect used DefaultValue as the *options* list, so when DefaultValue is empty
//    it would render no options.
// 2) MultiSelect didn'"'"'t show descriptions for rich options.
func main() {
	inv := &serpent.Invocation{}

	// Bug #1: list(string) options should still render even if DefaultValue is empty.
	p1 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
		Name:         "regions",
		Type:         "list(string)",
		DefaultValue: "[]",
		// In real usage, the available values are provided elsewhere; for this repo'"'"'s CLI implementation,
		// we now use `Options` as the available values source.
		Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
			{Name: "us-east", Value: "us-east"},

		},
	}

	// We can'"'"'t run the interactive UI in this repro. Instead, we verify the mapping logic
	// by calling the helper that converts rich options for MultiSelect.

	fmt.Println("lines:")
	for _, l := range lines {
		fmt.Println(" -", l)
	}
	b, _ := json.Marshal(values)
	fmt.Println("values_json:", string(b))
}

# We can'"'"'t run the Go TUI here easily, so we reproduce the core issues via:

# - verifying MultiSelect now supports rich options formatting (name + description) via helper
#
# This script expects the repo to have been fixed.

import json
import subprocess
import textwrap


def run(cmd):
    return subprocess.check_output(cmd, text=True)


def main():
    # Build a small Go snippet that calls the helper used by MultiSelect for rich options.
    go_src = textwrap.dedent(
        '"'"''"'"''"'"'
        package main

        import (
            "encoding/json"
            "fmt"

            "github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
            "github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
        )

        func main() {
            rich := []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
                {Name: "A", Value: "a", Description: "desc a"},
                {Name: "B", Value: "b"},
            }
            lines, values := cliui.MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(rich)
            b, _ := json.Marshal(values)
            fmt.Println("lines=", lines)
            fmt.Println("values=", string(b))
        }
        '"'"''"'"''"'"'
    )
    open('"'"'/testbed/_tmp_repro.go'"'"', '"'"'w'"'"').write(go_src)
    out = run(['"'"'bash'"'"', '"'"'-lc'"'"', '"'"'cd /testbed && go run ./_tmp_repro.go'"'"'])
    print(out)

    assert "A: desc a" in out, "expected rich option description to be included"
    assert '"'"'"a"'"'"' in out and '"'"'"b"'"'"' in out, "expected values to be correct"

    print("OK")


if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    main()
'

			// Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
			_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

			// For list(string) parameters, the available values come from the rich options.
			// The default selections come from `defaultValue` (which may be unset/empty).
			// Previously, we incorrectly used DefaultValue as the *options list*, which meant
			// no options were shown when DefaultValue was empty.
			available, _ := MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(templateVersionParameter.Options)

			var defaults []string
			if strings.TrimSpace(defaultValue) != "" {
				err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(defaultValue), &defaults)
				if err != nil {
					return "", err
				}
			}

			values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
				Options:  available,
				Defaults: defaults,
			})'

`json.Unmarshal(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue, &options)`\n  - then calls `MultiSelect` with `Options: options, Defaults: options`\n\nSo **the available options list is derived from `DefaultValue`**, which is wrong:\n- If `DefaultValue` is unset/empty/`[]`, the rendered list is empty → “MultiSelect does not present available options…”\n\nAlso, `MultiSelect` in `cli/cliui/select.go` only accepts `[]string` options, so it **cannot show rich option descriptions** (unlike `RichSelect` which formats `Name: Description`).\n\n### Intended minimal fix (what should be implemented)\nIf you apply this patch in a working environment, it should satisfy both PR bullets:\n\n1) **Don’t use DefaultValue as the options list** for `list(string)` parameters.\n   - Use `templateVersionParameter.Options` (rich options) as the *available* list.\n   - Parse `defaultValue` JSON array into `Defaults` only.\n\n2) **Support descriptions in MultiSelect** by formatting rich options like `RichSelect` does (`Name: Description`) and mapping selection back to `Value`.\n\nConcretely:\n\n#### A) Add a helper in `cli/cliui/select.go`\nAdd something like:\n\n```go\n// MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions converts rich options into display lines and a line->value map.\nfunc MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(rich []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption) (lines []string, lineToValue map[string]string) {\n\tlineToValue = make(map[string]string, len(rich))\n\tlines = make([]string, 0, len(rich))\n\n\tfor _, opt := range rich {\n\t\tline := opt.Name\n\t\tif strings.TrimSpace(opt.Description) != "" {\n\t\t\tline += ": " + opt.Description\n\t\t}\n\t\tlines = append(lines, line)\n\t\tlineToValue[line] = opt.Value\n\t}\n\treturn lines, lineToValue\n}\n```\n\n(You’ll need to import `github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk` and ensure `strings` is already imported there—it is.)\n\n#### B) Update `cli/cliui/parameter.go` list(string) branch\nReplace the current logic that unmarshals `templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue` into `options`.\n\nNew behavior should be:\n\n- `availableLines, lineToValue := MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(templateVersionParameter.Options)`\n- Parse `defaultValue` JSON array into `defaults []string` (if empty/blank → defaults stays empty).\n- Convert defaults (values) into display lines so MultiSelect highlights correctly:\n  - Build `defaultLineSet` by matching default values to rich options’ values and using the corresponding display line.\n- Call `MultiSelect` with:\n  - `Options: availableLines`\n  - `Defaults: defaultLines`\n- After selection returns display lines, map them back to option `Value` using `lineToValue`, falling back to raw line if not found (for safety / custom values).\n\nThat ensures:\n- Available options are shown even when default is empty.\n- Descriptions are visible in MultiSelect.\n- Returned JSON is of the selected *values* (not “Name: Description”).\n\n### Repro script idea (I started this)\nI started writing a small non-interactive repro (`/testbed/repro_multiselect.py`) that compiles a tiny Go snippet calling `MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions`, but I couldn’t finish validating it because the environment stopped returning output.\n\n---\n\nIf you can restore tool output (or re-run this in a fresh session), I can provide the exact minimal diffs applied to the repo and verify by running the repro script and `go test ./...`.', refusal=None, role='assistant', annotations=[], audio=None, function_call=None, tool_calls=None), content_filter_results={'protected_material_text': {'filtered': False, 'detected': False}})], created=1766679697, model='gpt-5.2-2025-12-11', object='chat.completion', service_tier=None, system_fingerprint=None, usage=CompletionUsage(completion_tokens=890, prompt_tokens=51533, total_tokens=52423, completion_tokens_details=CompletionTokensDetails(accepted_prediction_tokens=0, audio_tokens=0, reasoning_tokens=0, rejected_prediction_tokens=0), prompt_tokens_details=PromptTokensDetails(audio_tokens=0, cached_tokens=0)), prompt_filter_results=[{'prompt_index': 0, 'content_filter_results': {'jailbreak': {'filtered': False, 'detected': False}}}])

2025-12-26 00:30:25,154 - DEBUG - swea-lm - Response: ChatCompletion(id='chatcmpl-CqiVpXxVJN9uoXNiyHN22cVhAORPs', choices=[Choice(finish_reason='stop', index=0, logprobs=None, message=ChatCompletionMessage(content='I ran into a hard blocker with the execution environment partway through the fix: after editing, **all tool outputs became empty**, including `bash` (even `echo test` produced no output) and the file viewer. That means I can’t reliably (a) confirm file contents, (b) run the repro script, or (c) run `go test` to ensure the repository builds and tests pass.\n\nGiven that limitation, here’s the **minimal code change that should satisfy the PR requirements**, along with what still needs to be applied/verified once tool output is working again.\n\n---\n\n## What needs to change (minimal + correct)\n\n### Bug 1: `MultiSelect` skips options if default isn’t set (or is `[]`)\nRoot cause is in `cli/cliui/parameter.go` in the `list(string)` branch: it incorrectly treats `DefaultValue` as both:\n- the **available options** list, and\n- the **defaults** list.\n\nSo if `DefaultValue == "[]"` or empty, there are no available options shown.\n\n**Fix:** use `templateVersionParameter.Options` as the available options, and parse `defaultValue` JSON array as the defaults.\n\n### Bug 2: `MultiSelect` ignores descriptions\n`MultiSelect` currently accepts `[]string`, so when rich options exist (`[]TemplateVersionParameterOption`), descriptions are lost.\n\n**Fix:** format each option line as `"Name: Description"` (like `RichSelect` already does), but ensure selection returns the *Value* (not the combined string). That requires mapping display-line → value.\n\n---\n\n## Concrete implementation approach\n\n### 1) Add a helper to format rich options for MultiSelect\n\nAdd this function somewhere accessible in `cli/cliui/select.go` (or a small new file in the same package):\n\n```go\n// MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions converts rich options into display lines and a value mapping.\n// lines[i] is what is displayed; values[i] is the actual option Value (or Name if Value is empty).\nfunc MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(opts []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption) (lines []string, values []string) {\n\tlines = make([]string, 0, len(opts))\n\tvalues = make([]string, 0, len(opts))\n\n\tfor _, o := range opts {\n\t\tline := o.Name\n\t\tif strings.TrimSpace(o.Description) != "" {\n\t\t\tline += ": " + o.Description\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tval := o.Value\n\t\tif val == "" {\n\t\t\t// fallback for safety (some callers use Name-only options)\n\t\t\tval = o.Name\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlines = append(lines, line)\n\t\tvalues = append(values, val)\n\t}\n\n\treturn lines, values\n}\n```\n\nThis directly addresses “MultiSelect ignores descriptions”.\n\n### 2) Update `RichParameter` list(string) logic to use available options, not default\n\nIn `cli/cliui/parameter.go` `case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)"`:\n\n- Build available options from `templateVersionParameter.Options` via the helper above\n- Parse `defaultValue` JSON array into `defaults []string`\n- Call `MultiSelect` with:\n  - `Options: availableLines`\n  - `Defaults: ???` **must match what MultiSelect compares against**.\n\nTo make that work, MultiSelect must toggle by comparing the displayed string OR we map defaults to display strings. The clean approach is:\n\n### 3) Introduce a “rich” MultiSelect wrapper that returns values\n\nAdd a wrapper function:\n\n```go\nfunc RichMultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts RichSelectOptions, defaults []string) ([]string, error) {\n\tlines, values := MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(opts.Options)\n\n\t// Convert defaults (which are Values) into the displayed lines used by MultiSelect.\n\tdefaultLineSet := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor i, v := range values {\n\t\tfor _, d := range defaults {\n\t\t\tif v == d {\n\t\t\t\tdefaultLineSet[lines[i]] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tdefaultLines := make([]string, 0, len(defaultLineSet))\n\tfor l := range defaultLineSet {\n\t\tdefaultLines = append(defaultLines, l)\n\t}\n\n\tchosenLines, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{\n\t\tOptions:  lines,\n\t\tDefaults: defaultLines,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// Convert chosen display lines back to values.\n\tout +package main
+
+import (
+"encoding/json"
+"fmt"
+
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
+"github.com/coder/serpent"
+)
+
+// This is a minimal repro for the two bugs described:
+// 1) list(string) MultiSelect used DefaultValue as the *options* list, so when DefaultValue is empty
+//    it would render no options.
+// 2) MultiSelect didn't show descriptions for rich options.
+func main() {
+inv := &serpent.Invocation{}
+
+// Bug #1: list(string) options should still render even if DefaultValue is empty.
+p1 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:         "regions",
+Type:         "list(string)",
+DefaultValue: "[]",
+// In real usage, the available values are provided elsewhere; for this repo's CLI implementation,
+// we now use `Options` as the available values source.
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "us-east", Value: "us-east"},
+{Name: "us-west", Value: "us-west"},
+},
+}
+
+// We can't run the interactive UI in this repro. Instead, we verify the mapping logic
+// by calling the helper that converts rich options for MultiSelect.
+lines, values := cliui.MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(p1.Options)
+fmt.Println("lines:")
+for _, l := range lines {
+fmt.Println(" -", l)
+}
+b, _ := json.Marshal(values)
+fmt.Println("values_json:", string(b))
+}

+# Non-interactive repro of the MultiSelect-related bugs.
+#
+# We can't run the Go TUI here easily, so we reproduce the core issues via:
+# - verifying the old list(string) implementation incorrectly used DefaultValue as the options list
+# - verifying MultiSelect now supports rich options formatting (name + description) via helper
+#
+# This script expects the repo to have been fixed.
+
+import json
+import subprocess
+import textwrap
+
+
+def run(cmd):
+    return subprocess.check_output(cmd, text=True)
+
+
+def main():
+    # Build a small Go snippet that calls the helper used by MultiSelect for rich options.
+    go_src = textwrap.dedent(
+        '''
+        package main
+
+        import (
+            "encoding/json"
+            "fmt"
+
+            "github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
+            "github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
+        )
+
+        func main() {
+            rich := []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+                {Name: "A", Value: "a", Description: "desc a"},
+                {Name: "B", Value: "b"},
+            }
+            lines, values := cliui.MultiSelectLinesFromRichOptions(rich)
+            b, _ := json.Marshal(values)
+            fmt.Println("lines=", lines)
+            fmt.Println("values=", string(b))
+        }
+        '''
+    )
+    open('/testbed/_tmp_repro.go', 'w').write(go_src)
+    out = run(['bash', '-lc', 'cd /testbed && go run ./_tmp_repro.go'])
+    print(out)
+
+    assert "A: desc a" in out, "expected rich option description to be included"
+    assert '"a"' in out and '"b"' in out, "expected values to be correct"
+
+    print("OK")
+
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    main()
